components:\\n\\n## Event Creation\\nWhen a DOM event is dispatched, EventDispatcher::CreateEvent() in dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp creates the appropriate DOM Event object (e.g., MouseEvent, ClickEvent, etc.) wrapping the underlying WidgetEvent. The Event.h/cpp files define the base Event class that all DOM events inherit from.\\n\\n## Event Target Identification and Chain Building\\nThe process starts in EventDispatcher::Dispatch() in dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp, which:\\n1. Takes an event target (aTarget) and a WidgetEvent\\n2. Creates the initial EventTargetChainItem for the target via EventTargetChainItem::Create()\\n3. Builds the event target chain by iteratively calling EventTarget::GetEventTargetParent() (defined as pure virtual in dom/events/EventTarget.h)\\n4. Each target's GetEventTargetParent() implementation (e.g., nsIContent::GetEventTargetParent() in dom/base/FragmentOrElement.cpp) determines its parent in the chain\\n5. The chain continues until no parent target exists\\n\\nFor element nodes, FragmentOrElement.cpp contains nsIContent::GetEventTargetParent() which:\\n- Sets mCanHandle to indicate if the target can handle the event\\n- Identifies the parent target (either assigned slot or parent node)\\n- Handles shadow DOM retargeting and chrome-only access boundaries\\n- Determines event retargeting for related targets\\n\\n## Capture/Bubble Phase Traversal\\nEventTargetChainItem::HandleEventTargetChain() in dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp implements the W3C phase traversal:\\n1. **Capture Phase**: Iterates from the top of the chain downward (reverse order), calling HandleEvent on each target\\n   - Sets mInCapturePhase=true, mInBubblingPhase=false\\n   - Handles event retargeting and related target adjustments\\n2. **Target Phase**: Executes listeners on the actual target\\n   - Sets mInTargetPhase=true\\n   - Calls HandleEvent twice (once for capture, once for bubble)\\n3. **Bubble Phase**: Iterates from the target upward, calling HandleEvent on each ancestor\\n   - Sets mInBubblingPhase=true, mInCapturePhase=false\\n   - Only bubbles if event.bubbles=true\\n4. **System Event Group**: Re-dispatches through the same chain for system event group listeners\\n\\n## Event Listener Invocation\\nEventListenerManager::HandleEvent() in dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp:\\n1. Retrieves the EventListenerManager from each target via GetOrCreateListenerManager()\\n2. Filters listeners by phase (capture or bubble) based on event.eventPhase\\n3. Calls each matching listener's callback function\\n4. Respects listener flags like {capture, passive, once, inSystemGroup}\\n5. Updates cancelability and propagation flags based on listener responses\\n\\nThe EventListenerManager maintains separate listener lists for default event group and system event group, ensuring system listeners are invoked only during the system group dispatch.\\n\\n## Default Action Execution\\nAfter listener dispatch, PostHandleEvent() virtual methods are called (defined in EventTarget.h):\\n- nsINode::PostHandleEvent() in dom/base/nsINode.cpp provides base implementation\\n- Element::PostHandleEventForLinks() in dom/base/Element.cpp handles default actions for link elements\\n- nsGenericHTMLElement::PostHandleEventForAnchors() in dom/html/nsGenericHTMLElement.cpp delegates to PostHandleEventForLinks\\n\\nFor click events on anchor elements, Element::PostHandleEventForLinks() in dom/base/Element.cpp:\\n1. Checks if the event is a click (ePointerClick message)\\n2. Validates preconditions (link has href, not prevented by default, etc.)\\n3. Executes the default action: navigating to the href via nsContentUtils::TriggerLinkClick()\\n4. Sets mEventStatus to eConsumeNoDefault to prevent other default actions\\n5. Dispatches legacy DOMActivate event if needed\\n\\nThe entire dispatch flow is orchestrated in EventDispatcher::Dispatch() which:\\n1. Creates the event target chain\\n2. Initializes event properties (target, originalTarget, relatedTarget)\\n3. Calls EventTargetChainItem::HandleEventTargetChain() for both default and system event groups\\n4. Applies event retargeting rules for shadow DOM boundaries\\n5. Manages the isBeingDispatched flag to prevent recursive dispatches\\n6. Handles automatic chrome event dispatch and content dispatch control flags\\n\\nAll phases respect stopPropagation() and preventDefault() calls, allowing JavaScript to control event flow and prevent default actions.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":4,"cache_creation_input_tokens":360,"cache_read_input_tokens":64517,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":360},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"20cac3cb-1eda-4ec4-9db6-17e29d80e1cf","uuid":"625e559f-0793-4aa2-8ed8-674153c1325e"}

The Event.h/cpp files define the base Event class that all DOM events inherit from.\\n\\n## Event Target Identification and Chain Building\\nThe process starts in EventDispatcher::Dispatch() in dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp, which:\\n1. Takes an event target (aTarget) and a WidgetEvent\\n2. Creates the initial EventTargetChainItem for the target via EventTargetChainItem::Create()\\n3. Builds the event target chain by iteratively calling EventTarget::GetEventTargetParent() (defined as pure virtual in dom/events/EventTarget.h)\\n4. Each target's GetEventTargetParent() implementation (e.g., nsIContent::GetEventTargetParent() in dom/base/FragmentOrElement.cpp) determines its parent in the chain\\n5. The chain continues until no parent target exists\\n\\nFor element nodes, FragmentOrElement.cpp contains nsIContent::GetEventTargetParent() which:\\n- Sets mCanHandle to indicate if the target can handle the event\\n- Identifies the parent target (either assigned slot or parent node)\\n- Handles shadow DOM retargeting and chrome-only access boundaries\\n- Determines event retargeting for related targets\\n\\n## Capture/Bubble Phase Traversal\\nEventTargetChainItem::HandleEventTargetChain() in dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp implements the W3C phase traversal:\\n1. **Capture Phase**: Iterates from the top of the chain downward (reverse order), calling HandleEvent on each target\\n   - Sets mInCapturePhase=true, mInBubblingPhase=false\\n   - Handles event retargeting and related target adjustments\\n2. **Target Phase**: Executes listeners on the actual target\\n   - Sets mInTargetPhase=true\\n   - Calls HandleEvent twice (once for capture, once for bubble)\\n3. **Bubble Phase**: Iterates from the target upward, calling HandleEvent on each ancestor\\n   - Sets mInBubblingPhase=true, mInCapturePhase=false\\n   - Only bubbles if event.bubbles=true\\n4. **System Event Group**: Re-dispatches through the same chain for system event group listeners\\n\\n## Event Listener Invocation\\nEventListenerManager::HandleEvent() in dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp:\\n1. Calls each matching listener's callback function\\n4. Respects listener flags like {capture, passive, once, inSystemGroup}\\n5. Updates cancelability and propagation flags based on listener responses\\n\\nThe EventListenerManager maintains separate listener lists for default event group and system event group, ensuring system listeners are invoked only during the system group dispatch.\\n\\n## Default Action Execution\\nAfter listener dispatch, PostHandleEvent() virtual methods are called (defined in EventTarget.h):\\n- nsINode::PostHandleEvent() in dom/base/nsINode.cpp provides base implementation\\n- Element::PostHandleEventForLinks() in dom/base/Element.cpp handles default actions for link elements\\n- nsGenericHTMLElement::PostHandleEventForAnchors() in dom/html/nsGenericHTMLElement.cpp delegates to PostHandleEventForLinks\\n\\nFor click events on anchor elements, Element::PostHandleEventForLinks() in dom/base/Element.cpp:\\n1. Checks if the event is a click (ePointerClick message)\\n2. Validates preconditions (link has href, not prevented by default, etc.)\\n3. Executes the default action: navigating to the href via nsContentUtils::TriggerLinkClick()\\n4. Sets mEventStatus to eConsumeNoDefault to prevent other default actions\\n5. Dispatches legacy DOMActivate event if needed\\n\\nThe entire dispatch flow is orchestrated in EventDispatcher::Dispatch() which:\\n1. Creates the event target chain\\n2. Initializes event properties (target, originalTarget, relatedTarget)\\n3. Calls EventTargetChainItem::HandleEventTargetChain() for both default and system event groups\\n4.
